           <div class="article article-large cleared" data-original-title="What is a 'life interest trust' over a family home and what are a trustee's duties?" itemprop="itemListElement" itemscope="" itemtype="//schema.org/ListItem">
            <meta content="1" itemprop="position"/>
            <h2 class="linkro-darkred">
             <a href="/money/pensions/article-5966805/What-life-trust-family-home-trustees-duties.html" itemprop="url">
              My late father created a 'life interest trust' for my mother over their home: I'm a trustee so what are my duties?
             </a>
            </h2>
            <a href="/money/pensions/article-5966805/What-life-trust-family-home-trustees-duties.html">
             <img alt="What is a 'life interest trust' over a family home and what are a trustee's duties?" data-src="https://i.dailymail.co.uk/i/newpix/2018/07/19/13/4E67609600000578-0-image-a-11_1532004156363.jpg" height="185" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7" width="308"/>
             <noscript>
              <img alt="What is a 'life interest trust' over a family home and what are a trustee's duties?" height="185" src="https://i.dailymail.co.uk/i/newpix/2018/07/19/13/4E67609600000578-0-image-a-11_1532004156363.jpg" width="308"/>
             </noscript>
            </a>
            <div class="articletext-holder">
             <p>
              My father died a few years ago and left everything to my mother. They both had wills written by a solicitor that left everything to each other, but they created a Life Interest Trust over the house. My sister and I are trustees and I’ve been told this means we meed to add our names to the title deeds. What does this mean and how does it work? Lawyer Lorraine Robinson replies.
             </p>

   l_facebookLinkChannel =  '/pages/This-is-Money/310555847252';

     });
     return false;
 }

          <h6>
           BUSINESS &amp; MARKETS
          </h6>
          <div>

       <div class="cleared lead-alpha">
        <div class="alpha">
         <div class="column-splitter">
          <div class="column-split first-column">
           <div class="article article-large cleared" data-original-title="FTSE LIVE: Foxtons knocked by subdued property market; London stocks plunge after the bell" itemprop="itemListElement" itemscope="" itemtype="//schema.org/ListItem">
            <meta content="9" itemprop="position"/>
            <h2 class="linkro-darkred">
             <a href="/money/markets/article-6005987/FTSE-LIVE-Foxtons-knocked-subdued-property-market-London-stocks-plunge-bell.html" itemprop="url">
              FTSE LIVE: Foxtons knocked by subdued property market; Ladbrokes owner GVC in new US gaming venture; London stocks plunge after the bell
             </a>
            </h2>
            <a href="/money/markets/article-6005987/FTSE-LIVE-Foxtons-knocked-subdued-property-market-London-stocks-plunge-bell.html">
             <img alt="FTSE LIVE: Foxtons knocked by subdued property market; London stocks plunge after the bell" data-src="https://i.dailymail.co.uk/i/newpix/2018/07/30/08/1B019C7900000514-0-image-a-3_1532934435096.jpg" height="185" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7" width="308"/>
             <noscript>
              <img alt="FTSE LIVE: Foxtons knocked by subdued property market; London stocks plunge after the bell" height="185" src="https://i.dailymail.co.uk/i/newpix/2018/07/30/08/1B019C7900000514-0-image-a-3_1532934435096.jpg" width="308"/>
             </noscript>
            </a>
            <div class="articletext-holder">
             <p>
              London-focused estate agent Foxtons has slumped to a half-year loss, after a 'sustained period of low activity levels' in the capital dented its bottom line. And GVC - which owns Ladbrokes and Coral - has entered into a joint venture with MGM Resorts to launch a sports betting and interactive gaming platform in the US.
             </p>

         <div class="article article-tri-headline" itemprop="itemListElement" itemscope="" itemtype="//schema.org/ListItem">
          <meta content="15" itemprop="position"/>
          <h2 class="linkro-darkred">
           <a href="/money/holidays/article-6002343/The-60m-currency-trap-never-convert-restaurant-bill-sterling-abroad.html" itemprop="url">
            'How I spent an hour fighting €18 extra fee...on a €42 bar bill': Why you should never convert your restaurant or shop bill into sterling when abroad
           </a>
          </h2>
          <div class="articletext">
           <a href="/money/holidays/article-6002343/The-60m-currency-trap-never-convert-restaurant-bill-sterling-abroad.html">
            <img alt="The £60m currency trap: Why you should never convert your restaurant bill into sterling" data-src="https://i.dailymail.co.uk/i/newpix/2018/07/29/10/4EA5D14B00000578-0-image-a-10_1532857284531.jpg" height="382" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7" width="636"/>
            <noscript>
             <img alt="The £60m currency trap: Why you should never convert your restaurant bill into sterling" height="382" src="https://i.dailymail.co.uk/i/newpix/2018/07/29/10/4EA5D14B00000578-0-image-a-10_1532857284531.jpg" width="636"/>
            </noscript>
           </a>
           <div>
            <p>
             British tourists could save themselves more than £60million in rip-off fees next month – by wising up to the biggest currency trap used by overseas firms. A week ago, we highlighted how consumers routinely lose out on poor exchange rates before they have even left home. But today, we expose the trick that dupes millions of holidaymakers every year while abroad. It is known as 'dynamic currency conversion'.
            </p>
           </div>
          </div>

          <h2 class="linkro-darkred">
           <a href="/money/news/article-6000007/Interest-rates-set-time-2009-economy-improves.html" itemprop="url">
            Interest rates set to rise for first time since 2009 as economy improves - but expert warns it could be tricky to hike them any further before Brexit
           </a>
          </h2>
          <div class="articletext">
           <a href="/money/news/article-6000007/Interest-rates-set-time-2009-economy-improves.html">
            <img alt="Interest rates set to rise above 0.5% for first time since 2009 as economy improves" data-src="https://i.dailymail.co.uk/i/newpix/2018/07/27/16/15E4D97600000514-0-image-a-27_1532707082437.jpg" height="382" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7" width="636"/>
            <noscript>
             <img alt="Interest rates set to rise above 0.5% for first time since 2009 as economy improves" height="382" src="https://i.dailymail.co.uk/i/newpix/2018/07/27/16/15E4D97600000514-0-image-a-27_1532707082437.jpg" width="636"/>
            </noscript>
           </a>
           <div>
            <p>
             If the Bank of England's nine policymakers do raise the base rate from 0.5% to 0.75% on Thursday, it would be the highest it has been since March 2009, when it was slashed from 1% to 0.5% to stem the financial crisis. The predictions come as doubt was cast on a possible hike earlier this month, after inflation held steady at 2.4%, instead of rising to 2.6% as per economists' expectations.
            </p>

           </a>
          </h2>

          <h2 class="linkro-darkred">
           <a href="/money/pensions/article-5958685/Parents-lose-future-state-pension-child-benefit-shambles.html" itemprop="url">
            Thousands of mums and dads are losing state pension - because they make innocent blunders in paperwork after their child's birth
           </a>
          </h2>
          <div class="articletext">
           <a href="/money/pensions/article-5958685/Parents-lose-future-state-pension-child-benefit-shambles.html">
            <img alt="Parents lose future state pension in child benefit 'shambles'" data-src="https://i.dailymail.co.uk/i/newpix/2018/07/20/15/4E6FCEEF00000578-0-image-a-13_1532098442818.jpg" height="382" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7" width="636"/>
            <noscript>
             <img alt="Parents lose future state pension in child benefit 'shambles'" height="382" src="https://i.dailymail.co.uk/i/newpix/2018/07/20/15/4E6FCEEF00000578-0-image-a-13_1532098442818.jpg" width="636"/>
            </noscript>
           </a>
           <div>
            <p>
             Parents are losing state pension for failing to fill in a form. Emma Maslin (pictured) could be nearly £20,000 out of pocket over a 20 year retirement.              </a>
            </h2>
            <div class="articletext">
             <a href="/money/comment/article-5991603/RACHEL-RICKARD-STRAUS-time-maximise-impact-investors.html">
              <img alt="" data-src="https://i.dailymail.co.uk/i/newpix/2018/07/25/16/4E8F6A2400000578-0-image-m-3_1532533429287.jpg" height="115" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7" width="154"/>

              </noscript>
             </a>
             <p>
              As consumers we endlessly battle to reduce our impact: take the train instead of driving, decline plastic straws, eat free range. As investors we can maximise our impact, using our cash to do good.

             <img alt="Households are being pressured into having smart meters fitted" height="382" src="https://i.dailymail.co.uk/i/newpix/2018/07/20/11/4E6E113E00000578-0-image-a-7_1532083313615.jpg" width="636"/>
            </noscript>
           </a>
           <div>
            <p>
             Thirty per cent of UK households also said they have been pressured by their energy provider into having a smart meter fitted into their home. Of those a third said they felt their energy firm gave them no other choice than to have the new device fitted.
            </p>
           </div>

          <h2 class="linkro-darkred">
           <a href="/money/news/article-1607881/When-UK-rates-rise.html" itemprop="url">
            What next for interest rates? Doubts cast on August rate rise after inflation holds steady
           </a>
          </h2>
          <div class="articletext">
           <a href="/money/news/article-1607881/When-UK-rates-rise.html">
            <img alt="When will UK interest rates rise?" data-src="https://i.dailymail.co.uk/i/newpix/2018/07/23/11/4E827E3E00000578-0-image-a-5_1532342492014.jpg" height="382" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7" width="636"/>
            <noscript>
             <img alt="When will UK interest rates rise?" height="382" src="https://i.dailymail.co.uk/i/newpix/2018/07/23/11/4E827E3E00000578-0-image-a-5_1532342492014.jpg" width="636"/>
            </noscript>
           </a>
           <div>
            <p>
             Doubts have been cast on whether interest rates will rise in August after inflation held steady at 2.4 per cent. Markets had been pricing in a potential rate rise at the Bank of England's August meeting and inflation report, with some economists forecasting that the monetary policy committee would be swayed by better economic data recently. However, weight has now been added to the case made by other analysts that the Bank would hold at 0.5 per cent and pursue a wait-and-see strategy.
            </p>
           </div>

         <div class="money item">
          <div class="bigpic-puff-double ccogr2 link-ccox" data-track-module="llg-62022682^bigpic_puff" data-track-selector="a:not(.comments-link, .videos-link, .share-link)" id="p-955">
           <h3 class="wogr6">
            MORTGAGE GUIDES
           </h3>
           <div class="content-container cleared">
            <div class="left-content-container">
             <div class="js-article">
              <span class="slant-small-t">
              </span>
              <a class="title" href="/money/mortgageshome/article-2263815/The-time-buyers-guide-getting-mortgage.html">
               The essential guide to getting a mortgage
              </a>
              <span class="slant-small-b">
              </span>
              <span class="description">
               How they work and what you need to know
              </span>
              <div class="article-icon-links-container" data-followbutton="ThisIsMoney">

          <div class="articletext">

           <div>

           <div class="article article-large cleared" data-original-title="What next for mortgage rates?" itemprop="itemListElement" itemscope="" itemtype="//schema.org/ListItem">
            <meta content="80" itemprop="position"/>
            <h2 class="linkro-darkred">
             <a href="/money/mortgageshome/article-1687576/What-mortgage-rates.html" itemprop="url">
              What next for mortgage rates: Should you lock in to a cheap fix now?
             </a>
            </h2>
            <a href="/money/mortgageshome/article-1687576/What-mortgage-rates.html">
             <img alt="What next for mortgage rates?" data-src="https://i.dailymail.co.uk/i/pix/2016/05/16/10/3104568000000578-0-image-a-1_1463389766574.jpg" height="185" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7" width="308"/>
             <noscript>
              <img alt="What next for mortgage rates?" height="185" src="https://i.dailymail.co.uk/i/pix/2016/05/16/10/3104568000000578-0-image-a-1_1463389766574.jpg" width="308"/>
             </noscript>
            </a>
            <div class="articletext-holder">
             <p>
              Borrowers are being offered a raft of cheap fixed rate mortgages as lenders attempt to lure them into remortgaging or buying a home. But HSBC has decided to buck the trend and launch a new rate mortgage that is a tracker instead. We pick out the best fixed and tracker rate mortgages and look at what next for rates.

           <div class="article article-large cleared" data-original-title="Ten tips for buy-to-let: Essential advice for property investment" itemprop="itemListElement" itemscope="" itemtype="//schema.org/ListItem">
            <meta content="81" itemprop="position"/>
            <h2 class="linkro-darkred">
             <a href="/money/mortgageshome/article-1596759/Ten-tips-buy-let.html" itemprop="url">
              Ten tips for buy-to-let: the essential advice for property investors
             </a>
            </h2>
            <a href="/money/mortgageshome/article-1596759/Ten-tips-buy-let.html">
             <img alt="Ten tips for buy-to-let: Essential advice for property investment" data-src="https://i.dailymail.co.uk/i/pix/2016/04/13/10/319612D800000578-0-image-a-2_1460540307867.jpg" height="185" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7" width="308"/>
             <noscript>
              <img alt="Ten tips for buy-to-let: Essential advice for property investment" height="185" src="https://i.dailymail.co.uk/i/pix/2016/04/13/10/319612D800000578-0-image-a-2_1460540307867.jpg" width="308"/>
             </noscript>
            </a>
            <div class="articletext-holder">
             <p>
              Buy-to-let is much tougher than it once was. A tax crackdown on buying properties and a tax raid on the rental income from owning them has seen to that. But for many Britons the idea of investing in property still appeals, as they trust bricks and mortar and may feel that they can add value to a property. Read our top ten buy-to-let tips
             </p>
